GT Equivalence Verification (BPG2)

GT: c0*P*sin(c1*t) + c2*P*exp(-c3*t)
Candidate formulas: 50

I need to determine if any candidate formula can be made equivalent to the GT:

**GT: `0.2569*P*sin(0.7218*t) + 0.1149*P*exp(-0.0304*t)`**

This has two terms: one is `P*sin(αt)` and the other is `P*exp(-βt)` where β > 0.

Let me analyze candidates systematically. The GT is a function of both P and t, linear in P, with no constant term, no t-linear term, and no P² terms.

**Key structural requirements:**
- Must be linear in P (no P², no constant terms independent of P)
- Must contain P*sin(αt) or equivalent
- Must contain P*exp(-βt) or equivalent

Let me check candidates that have both sin and exp terms with P dependence:

**Candidate 36: `P*c0*sin(c1*t + c2) + c3*exp(c4*t) + c5*t + c6`**
- First term: P*c0*sin(c1*t + c2) — good, can produce P*sin(αt) with phase
- But exp term isn't multiplied by P. The GT has P*exp(-βt), so this doesn't match unless c3=0, but then we lose the exp term.

**Candidate 37: `P*c0 + P*c1*sin(c2*t + c3) + c4*exp(c5*t) + c6*sin(c7*t + c8)`**
- Same issue: exp term not multiplied by P.

**Candidate 17: `P*c0 + P*c1*cos(c2*t + c3) + c4*exp(c5*t) + c6*sin(c7*t + c8)`**
- Same issue.

**Candidate 4: `P²*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2*cos(c3*t + c4) + c5*t + c6 + c7*exp(c8*t)`**
- exp not multiplied by P.

**Candidate 8: `P*c0*cos(c1*t + c2) + P*c3 + c4 + c5*t`**
- Using cos with phase shift: P*c0*cos(c1*t + c2) = P*c0*[cos(c2)cos(c1*t) - sin(c2)sin(c1*t)]. This gives P*sin and P*cos but not P*exp. Setting c4=c5=0 and c3 handles constant P term, but can't produce P*exp(-βt).

**Candidate 20: `P*c0*sin(c1*t + c2) + P*c3/(P + c4) + c5*t/(c6 + c7*exp(c8*t))`**
- P*c3/(P+c4): if c4=0, this becomes c3, a constant (not P-dependent as needed). Can't make it P*exp.

**Candidate 35: `P*c0*sin(c1*t + c2) + P*c3*exp(P*c4) + c5*sin(c6*t + c7) + c8*t`**
- P*c3*exp(P*c4): if c4=0, this becomes P*c3 (constant in t, not exp(-βt)).

**Candidate 26: `P*c0*t^c1 + c2*t + c3 + c4*exp(c5*t)*sin(c6*t + c7)`**
- P*c0*t^c1 can't become P*exp(-βt).

**Candidate 32: `P*c0*exp(P*c1) + c2*t + c3 + c4*exp(c5*t)*sin(c6*t + c7)`**
- P*c0*exp(P*c1) is not linear in P for general P.

**Candidate 7: `P*c0 + P*c1*cos(c2*t + c3) + c4*t + c5 + c6*sin(c7*t + c8)`**
- No exp term at all. Can't produce P*exp(-βt).

After exhaustive review, none of the candidates contain a term of the form `P*exp(c*t)` which is essential for matching the GT's `P*exp(-0.0304*t)` term. The candidates either have exp terms not multiplied by P, or lack exp terms entirely. No algebraic manipulation of the available terms can produce `P*exp(-βt)` for all values of P and t.

[NO MATCH]

Conclusion: No match
